    + Use OpenJDK as is a lot smaller than Oracle Java

    + Remove swf unused video stuff
    + Remove XDummy xorg unused X stuff

    + Remove SEL_HOME and simply write /home/seluser

## v2.45.0-berlin
 + **Changes:** (2015-04-28)
